SQL> CREATE TABLE COUNTRY(Country_Name varchar(20), Population decimal(10,2), No_of_Worldcup_won NUMBER, Manager varchar(20), CONSTRAINT COUNTRY_PK PRIMARY KEY(Country_Name));

Table created.

SQL> CREATE TABLE PLAYERS(Player_id Number, Name varchar(40), Fname varchar(20), Lname varchar(35), DOB varchar(35), Country varchar(20), Height Number, Club varchar(30), Position varchar(10), Caps_for_Country Number, IS_CAPTAIN varchar(5), CONSTRAINT PLAYERS_PK PRIMARY KEY(Player_id), FOREIGN KEY(Country) REFERENCES COUNTRY(Country_Name));

Table created.

SQL> CREATE TABLE MATCH_RESULTS(Match_id Number, Date_of_Match varchar(35), Start_Time_of_Match varchar(35), Team1 varchar(25), Team2 varchar(25), Team1_Score Number, Team2_Score Number, Stadium_Name varchar(35),Host_City varchar(20), CONSTRAINT MATCH_RESULTS_PK PRIMARY KEY(Match_id), CONSTRAINT MATCH_RESULTS_FK FOREIGN KEY(Team1) REFERENCES COUNTRY(Country_Name), FOREIGN KEY(Team2) REFERENCES COUNTRY(Country_Name));

Table created.

SQL> CREATE TABLE PLAYER_CARDS(Player_id Number, Yellow_Cards Number, Red_Cards Number, CONSTRAINT PLAYER_CARDS_PK PRIMARY KEY(Player_id), CONSTRAINT PLAYER_CARDS_FK FOREIGN KEY(Player_id) REFERENCES PLAYERS(Player_id));

Table created.

SQL> CREATE TABLE PLAYER_ASSISTS_GOALS(Player_id Number,No_of_Matches Number,Goals Number,Assists Number,Minutes_Played Number,CONSTRAINT PLAYER_ASSISTS_GOALS_PK PRIMARY KEY(Player_id), CONSTRAINT PLAYER_ASSISTS_GOALS_FK FOREIGN KEY(Player_id) REFERENCES PLAYERS(Player_id));
